												'eventCategory': arguments[2],
												'eventLabel': arguments[4],
												'value': arguments[5] ? arguments[5] : 1,
											}
										}
									}
									if ('pageview' === arguments[1]) {
										if ('undefined' !== typeof arguments[2]) {
											hitObject = {
												'eventAction': 'page_view',
												'page_path': arguments[2],
											}
										}
									}
									if (typeof arguments[2] === 'object') {
										hitObject = arguments[2];
									}
									if (typeof arguments[5] === 'object') {
										Object.assign(hitObject, arguments[5]);
									}
									if ('undefined' !== typeof arguments[1].hitType) {
										hitObject = arguments[1];
										if ('pageview' === hitObject.hitType) {
											hitObject.eventAction = 'page_view';
										}
									}
									if (hitObject) {
										action = 'timing' === arguments[1].hitType ? 'timing_complete' : hitObject.eventAction;
										hitConverted = mapArgs(hitObject);
										__gtagTracker('event', action, hitConverted);
									}
								}
								return;
							}

							function mapArgs(args) {
								var arg, hit = {};
								var gaMap = {
									'eventCategory': 'event_category',
									'eventAction': 'event_action',
									'eventLabel': 'event_label',
									'eventValue': 'event_value',
									'nonInteraction': 'non_interaction',
									'timingCategory': 'event_category',
									'timingVar': 'name',
									'timingValue': 'value',
									'timingLabel': 'event_label',
									'page': 'page_path',
									'location': 'page_location',
									'title': 'page_title',
									'referrer' : 'page_referrer',
								};
								for (arg in args) {
																		if (!(!args.hasOwnProperty(arg) || !gaMap.hasOwnProperty(arg))) {
										hit[gaMap[arg]] = args[arg];
									} else {
										hit[arg] = args[arg];
									}
								}
								return hit;
							}

							try {
								f.hitCallback();
							} catch (ex) {
							}
						};
						__gaTracker.create = newtracker;
						__gaTracker.getByName = newtracker;
						__gaTracker.getAll = function () {
							return [];
						};
						__gaTracker.remove = noopfn;
						__gaTracker.loaded = true;
						window['__gaTracker'] = __gaTracker;
					})();
									} else {
										console.log("");
					(function () {
						function __gtagTracker() {
							return null;
						}

						window['__gtagTracker'] = __gtagTracker;
						window['gtag'] = __gtagTracker;
					})();
									}
			</script>

									<section id="hard-rock-games-seo"><center>
<h3>Free Slots, Jackpots, Blackjack and Match-3 the Hard Rock Way</h3>
<a href="https://www.hardrockgames.com/">Hard Rock Games</a> brings you a lineup built to stand out. Spin <a href="https://www.hardrockgames.com/games/">free slots</a> packed with bonus rounds, wild features, and massive virtual jackpot wins. Hit classic blackjack and casino table games in <a href="https://www.hardrockgames.com/games/blackjack-casino-table-games/">Hard Rock Blackjack &amp; Casino</a>, or swipe through rock-inspired match-3 puzzle levels in <a href="https://www.hardrockgames.com/games/adventures-match-3-puzzle/">Hard Rock Adventures</a>. Every Hard Rock social casino app leans into what players actually want: free play, fresh content, and big in-game wins.</center><center><br />
<h3>A Connected World of Free-to-Play Hard Rock Casino Apps</h3>
The <a href="https://www.hardrockgames.com/games/">Hard Rock Games collection</a> includes <a href="https://www.hardrockgames.com/games/neverland-casino-slots/">Hard Rock Neverland Casino</a>, <a href="https://www.hardrockgames.com/games/hard-rock-jackpot-planet/">Hard Rock Jackpot Planet</a>, <a href="https://www.hardrockgames.com/games/jackpot-casino-games/">Hard Rock Jackpot Casino</a>, <a href="https://www.hardrockgames.com/games/seminole-slots-casino/">Seminole Social Casino</a>, <a href="https://www.hardrockgames.com/games/blackjack-casino-table-games/">Hard Rock Blackjack &amp; Casino</a>, and <a href="https://www.hardrockgames.com/games/adventures-match-3-puzzle/">Hard Rock Adventures</a>. Together they create a full universe of free-to-play social casino apps filled with Vegas-style slots, jackpot games, blackjack 21, roulette, poker, and match-3 puzzle challenges. Wdollars tie the experience together as a shared virtual currency, letting you earn and spend across participating Hard Rock titles.</center><center>
<h3> </h3>
<h3>Clans, Missions, Collectible Cards and Albums</h3>
Hard Rock Games is built for players who want more than spinning reels. Join clans to team up with other players, chase clan milestones, and compete in group events. Crush missions to earn Wdollars, bonus spins, and unlock new features in your favorite free slots and casino games. Collect limited-time cards, complete themed albums, and hit milestones that unlock jackpots, boosters, and extra rewards across the <a href="https://www.hardrockgames.com/games/">Hard Rock Games</a> lineup.</center><center>
<h3> </h3>
<h3>More Ways to Play, More Events to Hit, All Free</h3>
Every app in the Hard Rock universe drops new features, slots, game modes, and social events. Check the latest <a href="https://www.hardrockgames.com/game-updates/">game updates</a> to see new Konami slots, VIP games, seasonal themes, and fresh mechanics like battles and tournaments. All gameplay stays free-to-play with optional in-app purchases, so you can enjoy online casino-style entertainment without gambling at a real money casino.</center><center>
<h3> </h3>
<h3>Giveaways, Real Winners and Big-Moment Drops</h3>
Hard Rock Games keeps the action going with ongoing <a href="https://www.hardrockgames.com/giveaways/">giveaways</a>, Unity point events, and special promotions that reward players for logging in and playing free slots, blackjack, and match-3 puzzle games. Every month, real players across the U.S. and Canada score cash, gift cards, Unity rewards and more. Visit the <a href="https://www.hardrockgames.com/winners-hub-page/">Giveaway Winners hub</a> to see the latest winners, then jump into your favorite Hard Rock casino apps to stack entries and chase the next big moment.</center><center>
<h3> </h3>
<h3>Our Most Popular Hard Rock Social Casino Slots</h3>

					const lazyloadBackgroundObserver = new IntersectionObserver( ( entries ) => {
						entries.forEach( ( entry ) => {

								let lazyloadBackground = entry.target;
								if( lazyloadBackground ) {
									lazyloadBackground.classList.add( 'e-lazyloaded' );
								}
								lazyloadBackgroundObserver.unobserve( entry.target );
							}
						});
